# Available API Events - Wisp Forest Docs

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/api_events/#accessorychangecallback)

Available API Events
====================

### [AccessoryChangeCallback](https://github.com/wisp-forest/accessories/blob/fa06f044f5c7486b26a8c0774f7ca3edbd256cad/common/src/main/java/io/wispforest/accessories/api/events/AccessoryChangeCallback.java#L15)
[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/api_events/#accessorychangecallback "Permanent link")

An event which fires when a change for a slot occurs. The event provides the current stack, and the previous stack combined with the type of slot change which occurred. That change can either be `MUTATION` or `REPLACEMENT`.

*   `MUTATION` means that the stack was not unequipped but the NBT data was modified. Usually it is still the same item.
*   `REPLACEMENT` indicates a `setStack()` call has occurred on the inventory, leading to the stack being entirely different (usually or always?).

### [AdjustAttributeModifierCallback](https://github.com/wisp-forest/accessories/blob/fa06f044f5c7486b26a8c0774f7ca3edbd256cad/common/src/main/java/io/wispforest/accessories/api/events/AdjustAttributeModifierCallback.java#L16)
[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/api_events/#adjustattributemodifiercallback "Permanent link")

An event used to adjust the attributes of the accessory stack. This is collected from the [DataComponent method](https://github.com/wisp-forest/accessories/blob/a549372f7b6ac9a367d1b49a821759528cadce24/common/src/main/java/io/wispforest/accessories/api/components/AccessoryItemAttributeModifiers.java#L45)
 or from the [`Accessory#getModifiers`](https://github.com/wisp-forest/accessories/blob/a549372f7b6ac9a367d1b49a821759528cadce24/common/src/main/java/io/wispforest/accessories/api/Accessory.java#L81)
 call.

### [AllowEntityModificationCallback](https://github.com/wisp-forest/accessories/blob/fa06f044f5c7486b26a8c0774f7ca3edbd256cad/common/src/main/java/io/wispforest/accessories/api/events/AllowEntityModificationCallback.java#L22)
[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/api_events/#allowentitymodificationcallback "Permanent link")

An event used for allowing or restricting access for an entity to modify various aspects of Accessories. Some examples include opening the screen, adjusting accessories, or toggling the visibility of the rendering.

### [CanEquipCallback](https://github.com/wisp-forest/accessories/blob/fa06f044f5c7486b26a8c0774f7ca3edbd256cad/common/src/main/java/io/wispforest/accessories/api/events/CanEquipCallback.java#L21)
[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/api_events/#canequipcallback "Permanent link")

An event used to adjust if the accessory is equippable based on the `ItemStack` and `SlotReference`

### [CanUnequipCallback](https://github.com/wisp-forest/accessories/blob/fa06f044f5c7486b26a8c0774f7ca3edbd256cad/common/src/main/java/io/wispforest/accessories/api/events/CanUnequipCallback.java#L15)
[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/api_events/#canunequipcallback "Permanent link")

An event used to adjust if the accessory can be unequipped based on the `ItemStack` and `SlotReference`

### [ContainersChangeCallback](https://github.com/wisp-forest/accessories/blob/fa06f044f5c7486b26a8c0774f7ca3edbd256cad/common/src/main/java/io/wispforest/accessories/api/events/ContainersChangeCallback.java#L17C18-L17C43)
[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/api_events/#containerschangecallback "Permanent link")

An event fired when a change occurs for the [AccessoryContainer](https://github.com/wisp-forest/accessories/blob/fa06f044f5c7486b26a8c0774f7ca3edbd256cad/common/src/main/java/io/wispforest/accessories/api/AccessoriesContainer.java#L13)
. This happens before the changes are synced. It provides a map of changed containers (`AccessoriesContainer`s) to whether the change was related to resizing (boolean).

### [OnDropCallback](https://github.com/wisp-forest/accessories/blob/fa06f044f5c7486b26a8c0774f7ca3edbd256cad/common/src/main/java/io/wispforest/accessories/api/events/OnDropCallback.java#L19)
[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/api_events/#ondropcallback "Permanent link")

An event used to adjust the drop rule for the stack when such is being handled after the of the target entity found within [`AccessoriesEventHandler#onDeath`](https://github.com/wisp-forest/accessories/blob/fa06f044f5c7486b26a8c0774f7ca3edbd256cad/common/src/main/java/io/wispforest/accessories/impl/AccessoriesEventHandler.java#L564)
.

### [OnDeathCallback](https://github.com/wisp-forest/accessories/blob/fa06f044f5c7486b26a8c0774f7ca3edbd256cad/common/src/main/java/io/wispforest/accessories/api/events/OnDeathCallback.java#L18)
[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/api_events/#ondeathcallback "Permanent link")

An event fired after an entity dies, and after all `OnDropCallback` have been calculated. This can be used to cancel default dropping behavior, or adjust stack data before dropping the items.

Implemented Events[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/api_events/#implemented-events "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Any event below can be implemented directly on an `Accessory` implementation or by registering to the event object within the respective interface.

### [AllowWalkingOnSnow](https://github.com/wisp-forest/accessories/blob/fa06f044f5c7486b26a8c0774f7ca3edbd256cad/common/src/main/java/io/wispforest/accessories/api/events/extra/AllowWalkingOnSnow.java#L20)
[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/api_events/#allowwalkingonsnow "Permanent link")

An event allowing the ability to adjust if the entity should be able to walk on powdered snow.

### [IsGazeDisguised](https://github.com/wisp-forest/accessories/blob/c41504c63f5c608e1e0ea249fae8b1a152c92f29/common/src/main/java/io/wispforest/accessories/api/events/extra/IsGazeDisguised.java#L20)
[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/api_events/#isgazedisguised "Permanent link")

An event allowing for the control over if the given looking `LivingEntity` sees the wearer entity as disguised to prevent certain actions like being angered or allowing the creature to move.

### [FortuneAdjustment](https://github.com/wisp-forest/accessories/blob/fa06f044f5c7486b26a8c0774f7ca3edbd256cad/common/src/main/java/io/wispforest/accessories/api/events/extra/FortuneAdjustment.java#L18)
[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/api_events/#fortuneadjustment "Permanent link")

An event allowing for the adjustment of the level of fortune provided to the entity when calculating for such.

### [LootingAdjustment](https://github.com/wisp-forest/accessories/blob/fa06f044f5c7486b26a8c0774f7ca3edbd256cad/common/src/main/java/io/wispforest/accessories/api/events/extra/LootingAdjustment.java#L17)
[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/api_events/#lootingadjustment "Permanent link")

An event allowing for the adjustment of the level of looting provided to the entity when calculating for on the death of an attacked entity.

### [PiglinNeutralInducer](https://github.com/wisp-forest/accessories/blob/fa06f044f5c7486b26a8c0774f7ca3edbd256cad/common/src/main/java/io/wispforest/accessories/api/events/extra/PiglinNeutralInducer.java#L19)
[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/api_events/#piglinneutralinducer "Permanent link")

An event allowing for adjusting if the entity should anger any piglins within range of them.

**Deprecated**[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/api_events/#deprecated "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [EndermanMasked](https://github.com/wisp-forest/accessories/blob/fa06f044f5c7486b26a8c0774f7ca3edbd256cad/common/src/main/java/io/wispforest/accessories/api/events/extra/EndermanMasked.java#L20)
[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/api_events/#endermanmasked "Permanent link")

Recommend switching to `IsGazeDisguised` event instead and specifically checking for Enderman as the looker entity.

* * *

Last update: 2024-12-19

[Back to top](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/api_events/#)

# Adding Wiki Sources - Wisp Forest Docs

 

Adding Wiki Sources
===================

The built-in **Wiki** (`limelight:wiki`) extension has support for custom wikis, defined via resource packs. Limelight addons can register custom wiki sources to add support for non-default types of wikis.

Let's add a wiki source for a hypothetical wiki that has an API like this:

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-0-1) GET https://wiki.example.com/api/search?query=funny [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-0-2) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-0-3) HTTP 200 [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-0-4) [ [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-0-5)     ["Funny Page", "https://wiki.example.com/funny"] [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-0-6) ]`

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-1) public record FunnyWikiSource(String apiUrl) implements WikiSource { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-2)     // (1) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-3)     public static final Endec<FunnyWikiSource> ENDEC = StructEndecBuilder.of( [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-4)         Endec.STRING.fieldOf("api_url", FunnyWikiSource::apiUrl), [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-5)         FunnyWikiSource::new [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-6)     ); [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-7) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-8)     public static final WikiSourceType<FunnyWikiSource> TYPE = new WikiSourceType<>(ENDEC); [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-9) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-10)     public static void init() { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-11)         Registry.register(WikiSourceType.REGISTRY, Identifier.of("example-extension", "funny"), TYPE); [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-12)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-13) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-14)     @Override [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-15)     public String createSearchUrl(String searchText) { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-16)         // (2) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-17)         return apiUrl + "/search?query=" + URLEncoder.encode(searchText, StandardCharsets.UTF_8); [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-18)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-19) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-20)     @Override [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-21)     public void gatherEntriesFromSearch(String queryBody, String searchText, Consumer<EntryData> entryConsumer) { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-22)         JsonArray json = JsonParser.parseString(queryBody).getAsJsonArray(); [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-23) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-24)         for (var resultEl : json) { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-25)             JsonArray result = resultEl.getAsJsonArray(); [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-26) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-27)             entryConsumer.accept(new EntryData(result.get(0).getAsString(), result.get(1).getAsString())); [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-28)         } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-29)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-30) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-31)     @Override [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-32)     public WikiSourceType<?> type() { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-33)         return TYPE; [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-34)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-1-35) }`

1.  This is an [Endec](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/owo/endec/)
    , oωo's serialization system.  
    If you prefer Codecs, you can use them too:
    
    `[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-2-1) public static final Codec<FunnyWikiSource> CODEC = RecordCodecBuilder.create(i -> i.group( [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-2-2)         Codec.STRING.fieldOf("api_url").forGetter(FunnyWikiSource::apiUrl) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-2-3)     ).apply(i, FunnyWikiSource::new) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-2-4) ); [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-2-5) public static final WikiSourceType<FunnyWikiSource> TYPE = new WikiSourceType<>(CODEC);`
    
2.  This method returns a URL that needs to be queried to find entries for this search text. If your wiki has a central search index, you can just always return that, since the retrieved contents will be cached.
    

After this source type is registered, you need to add your wiki[1](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#fn:1)
:

assets/example-extension/limelight/wiki/funny.json

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-3-1) { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-3-2)     "type": "example-extension:funny", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-3-3)     "title": "Funny!", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-3-4)     "bang_key": "funnywiki", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-3-5)     "source": { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-3-6)         "api_url": "https://wiki.example.com/api" [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-3-7)     }, [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-3-8)     "language_overrides": { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-3-9)         "en_pt": { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-3-10)             "api_url": "https://piratewiki.example.com/api" [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-3-11)         } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-3-12)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#__codelineno-3-13) }`

This results in this output: ![a search box with 'fun' typed in it. Funny Page is the first result](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/assets/limelight/custom_wiki_source_implicit.png) ![a search box with '!funnywiki fun' typed in it. Funny Page is the only result](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/assets/limelight/custom_wiki_source_explicit.png)

* * *

1.  The wiki format is described in the [Adding Wikis](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/configuring/adding_wikis/)
     page [↩](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#fnref:1 "Jump back to footnote 1 in the text")
    

* * *

Last update: 2024-08-30

[Back to top](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/adding_wiki_sources/#)

# Providing Results - Wisp Forest Docs

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#defining-results)

Providing Results
=================

Defining results[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#defining-results "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`ResultEntry` is the sealed base interface of all results in Limelight. While it has some common members between all result types, the actual logic is determined by its permitted subinterfaces.

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-0-1) public abstract class BaseFunnyResultEntry /* implements ResultEntry */ { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-0-2)     public LimelightExtension extension() { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-0-3)         return MyFunExtension.INSTANCE; // (1) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-0-4)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-0-5) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-0-6)     public String entryId() { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-0-7)         return "example-extension:funny"; // (2) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-0-8)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-0-9) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-0-10)     public Text text() { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-0-11)         return Text.literal("wow very funny"); [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-0-12)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-0-13) }`

1.  This should return whatever extension generated this result, to be shown to the user as the result's source.
    
2.  This identifier should include as much information about the result as possible, to allow Limelight to identify equivalent results.
    

### Invoking result entries[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#invoking-result-entries "Permanent link")

`InvokeResultEntry` represents a result that runs some generic action.

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-1-1) public class MeowResultEntry extends BaseFunnyResultEntry implements InvokeResultEntry { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-1-2)     @Override [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-1-3)     public void run() { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-1-4)         MinecraftClient.getInstance().player.sendMessage(Text.literal("meow!")); [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-1-5)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-1-6) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-1-7)     @Override [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-1-8)     public boolean closesScreen() { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-1-9)         return false; // (1) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-1-10)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-1-11) }`

1.  Entries should ideally close the screen if the user is likely to not want to run anything else after this entry (e.g. keybind entries).

![](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/assets/limelight/invoke_result_example.png)

### Set search text result entries[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#set-search-text-result-entries "Permanent link")

`SetSearchTextEntry` represents a result entry which is offered as an autocomplete suggestion or to just redirect to different search text. The Limelight GUI will also show the text to be autocompleted to in the search box while this entry is highlighted.

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-2-1) public class CompleteMeowResultEntry extends BaseFunnyResultEntry implements SetSearchTextEntry { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-2-2)     @Override [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-2-3)     public String newSearchText() { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-2-4)         return "meow"; [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-2-5)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-2-6) }`

![](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/assets/limelight/autocomplete_result_example.png)

### Toggle result entries[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#toggle-result-entries "Permanent link")

Warning

This result entry type is experimental, and may be removed in a future update.

`ToggleResultEntry` represents a toggleable result entry. The Limelight GUI includes a checkbox in this result's component, which is toggled when the entry is used.

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-3-1) public class ControlMeowResultEntry extends BaseFunnyResultEntry implements ToggleResultEntry { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-3-2)     private static boolean MEOW_CONTROLLED = false; [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-3-3) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-3-4)     @Override [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-3-5)     public boolean getValue() { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-3-6)         return MEOW_CONTROLLED; [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-3-7)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-3-8) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-3-9)     @Override [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-3-10)     public void setValue(boolean value) { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-3-11)         MEOW_CONTROLLED = value; [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-3-12)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-3-13) }`

![](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/assets/limelight/toggle_result_example.png)

Gathering results[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#gathering-results "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To get results to the user, you need to not only define the result classes, but also provide them to Limelight. `ResultEntryGatherer` is the main interface for providing any results to the Limelight screen, used everywhere where you can provide entries.

### Implicit providers[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#implicit-providers "Permanent link")

`LimelightExtension` extends `ResultEntryGatherer`, and the core result gatherer invokes all extensions' gatherers if no extension handles it exclusively.

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-4-1) public class MyFunExtension implements LimelightExtension { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-4-2)     // ... [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-4-3) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-4-4)     @Override [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-4-5)     public void gatherEntries(ResultGatherContext ctx, Consumer<ResultEntry> entryConsumer) { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-4-6)         if (!ctx.matches("meow", "kitty", "cat")) return; // (1) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-4-7)         entryConsumer.accept(new MeowResultEntry()); [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-4-8)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-4-9) }`

1.  Provided entries aren't checked against the search text (in part to allow extensions like the calculator to function), so entry providers need to check search text themselves.  
    `ResultGatherContext.matches` is provided for this purpose, and extension should give all possible text that could be searched for to the method to allow users to search for their entries.

### Exclusive providers[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#exclusive-providers "Permanent link")

Your extension might want to add custom search syntax that means "only let _this_ extension handle it". `LimelightExtension#checkExclusiveGatherer` is provided for this purpose: the extension can check the gather context and return a gatherer that will exclusively handle this search. This is used by the built-in calculator extension (for `=` queries) and the bangs extension (for `!` queries).

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-5-1) public class MyFunExtension implements LimelightExtension { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-5-2)     // ... [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-5-3) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-5-4)     @Override [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-5-5)     public @Nullable ResultEntryGatherer checkExclusiveGatherer(ResultGatherContext ctx) { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-5-6)         if (!ctx.searchText().startsWith("~")) return null; [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-5-7) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-5-8)         return (ctx1, entryConsumer) -> { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-5-9)             entryConsumer.accept(new MeowResultEntry()); [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-5-10)         }; [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-5-11)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-5-12) }`

### Bangs[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#bangs "Permanent link")

Note

This requires the built-in **Bangs** (`limelight:bangs`) extension to be enabled.

Bangs ([a very original idea](https://duckduckgo.com/bangs)
) can be used to let users quickly search for specific types of result entries.

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-6-1) public class MyFunExtension implements LimelightExtension, BangsProvider { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-6-2)     @Override [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-6-3)     public List<BangDefinition> bangs() { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-6-4)         return List.of(new BangDefinition( [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-6-5)             "meow", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-6-6)             Text.literal("Meow!"), [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-6-7)             (ctx, entryConsumer) -> { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-6-8)                 entryConsumer.accept(new MeowResultEntry()); [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-6-9)             } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-6-10)         )); [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-6-11)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-6-12) }`

![](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/assets/limelight/bangs_example.png)

### Asynchronous gathering[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#asynchronous-gathering "Permanent link")

While most of Limelight's (and probably yours) extensions provide results synchronously, Limelight has full support for gatherers which provide results asynchronously, after the initial gathering has finished and the initial results are visible.

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-7-1) public class MyFunExtension implements LimelightExtension { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-7-2)     @Override [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-7-3)     public void gatherEntries(ResultGatherContext ctx, Consumer<ResultEntry> entryConsumer) { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-7-4)         var future = [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-7-5)             ctx.cancellationToken().wrapFuture(doWork()) // (1) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-7-6)                 .thenAccept(value -> { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-7-7)                     if (value > 10) return; [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-7-8) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-7-9)                     entryConsumer.accept(new MeowResultEntry()); [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-7-10)                 }); [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-7-11) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-7-12)         ctx.trackFuture(future); // (2) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-7-13)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-7-14) [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-7-15)     private CompletableFuture<Integer> doWork() { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-7-16)         return new CompletableFuture<Integer>() [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-7-17)             .completeOnTimeout(4, 5, TimeUnit.SECONDS); [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-7-18)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#__codelineno-7-19) }`

1.  CancellationToken is an object similar to JavaScript's [AbortSignal](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/AbortSignal)
     and .NET's [CancellationToken](https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/dotnet/api/system.threading.cancellationtoken)
    . Here, it's used to represent the lifetime of this specific Limelight search, and it will be cancelled if the screen is closed or if the search text changes. `CancellationToken#wrapFuture` attaches a subscription that will cancel the future when the token is cancelled.
    
2.  This line makes the Limelight core track the future to show a progress indicator while it's running, and notify the user if it fails (**WIP**).
    

* * *

Last update: 2024-08-30

[Back to top](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/limelight/extending/providing_results/#)

# ItemStack Data Components - Wisp Forest Docs

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#general)

ItemStack Data Components
=========================

General[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#general "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Below is the current set of available Data Components for ItemStacks that are supported with documentation about their function and format.

### Attribute Modifiers[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#attribute-modifiers "Permanent link")

Any ItemStack can have Attributes added onto it with the `accessories:attributes` Item Component. It is composed from a list of attribute entries similar to Minecraft's default implementation. Below is an example:

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-0-1) { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-0-2)     "accessories:attributes": { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-0-3)         "modifiers": [ [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-0-4)             { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-0-5)                 "type": "minecraft:attack_damage", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-0-6)                 "id": "example:increased_damage_boost", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-0-7)                 "amount": 1, [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-0-8)                 "operation": "add_value", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-0-9)                 "slot_name": "hat", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-0-10)                 "is_stackable": false, [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-0-11)             } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-0-12)         ] [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-0-13)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-0-14) }`

| Field | Usage |
| --- | --- |
| `"type"` | Refers to the attribute type that should be adjusted with the given modifier data. This can either be a slot attribute or a registered slot. |
| `"id"` | The unique resource location to identify this modifier |
| `"amount"` | The amount of change from the modifier |
| `"operation"` | The type of calculation operation that should be performed out of the valid values. |
| `"slot_name"` | Specify a slot to add a strict requirement to where the accessory must be equipped for the effect to apply. Use `"any"` to allow for the attribute to be applied to whatever slot the given item can be equipped into. |
| `"is_stackable"` | Allows for additional copies of the attribute to function together as a compounding effect |

Stacking Attributes

If the given attribute entry is desired to be stacked with other equipped accessory it may be good to use `"is_stackable"` which indicates that the given `"id"` passed should be appended with slot information to allow.

### Slot Validation[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#slot-validation "Permanent link")

Any ItemStack can define invalid or valid slots to which it can be equipped to using the `accessories:slot_validation` Item Component. Using it allows you to add to or override the equipability for an existing Accessory.

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-1-1) { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-1-2)     "accessories:slot_validation": { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-1-3)         "valid_slot": [ [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-1-4)             "hat" [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-1-5)         ] [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-1-6)         "invalid_slot": [ [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-1-7)             "shoes" [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-1-8)         ] [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-1-9)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-1-10) }`

| Field | Usage |
| --- | --- |
| `"valid_slots"` | An array of string values of valid slots that the stack can be equipped into |
| `"invalid_slots"` | An array of string values of invalid slots that the stack **can not** be equipped into |

### Stack Size[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#stack-size "Permanent link")

This Data Component allows you to adjust the max stack size of an Item for a single Accessory Slot. This can be useful in cases where you want to only allow equipping a specific amount of items int it (E.G. heart containers, or consumables). Note that your size override must be **smaller** than the max stack size of the Item.

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-2-1) { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-2-2)     "accessories:stack_size": { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-2-3)         "use_stack_size": false, [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-2-4)         "size_override": 69 [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-2-5)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-2-6) }`

| Field | Usage |
| --- | --- |
| `"use_stack_size"` | Use the stack's given max size as the amount allowed to stack to within Accessories |
| `"size_override"` | The amount that the size should be overridden to instead of stack size |

### Accessory Nest[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#accessory-nest "Permanent link")

Accessories has a system that allows for nesting an Accessory within another Accessory. This can only be done explicitly with the API (code), or when creating a new ItemStack that has the `nested_accessories` Data Component. Example:

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-1) { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-2)     "accessories:nested_accessories": { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-3)         "accessories": [ [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-4)             { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-5)                 "id": "minecraft:diamond", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-6)                 "count": 1, [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-7)                 "components": { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-8)                     "accessories:attributes": { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-9)                         "modifiers": [ [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-10)                             { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-11)                                 "type": "minecraft:attack_damage", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-12)                                 "id": "example:increased_damage_boost", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-13)                                 "amount": 1, [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-14)                                 "operation": "add_value", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-15)                                 "slot_name": "any", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-16)                                 "is_stackable": false, [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-17)                             } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-18)                         ] [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-19)                     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-20)                 } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-21)             } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-22)             { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-23)                 "id": "minecraft:emerald", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-24)                 "count": 1, [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-25)                 "components": { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-26)                     "accessories:attributes": { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-27)                         "modifiers": [ [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-28)                             { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-29)                                 "type": "minecraft:attack_speed", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-30)                                 "id": "example:increased_damage_speed", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-31)                                 "amount": 1, [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-32)                                 "operation": "add_value", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-33)                                 "slot_name": "any", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-34)                                 "is_stackable": false, [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-35)                             } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-36)                         ] [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-37)                     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-38)                 } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-39)             } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-40)         ] [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-41)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-3-42) }`

| Field | Usage |
| --- | --- |
| `"accessories"` | A list of `ItemStack`s that have various components and will be used to get Accessory info from when equipping the nest |

Nest Equipability

Make sure to remember the equipability of your nest. If your Nested Accessory needs to change its equipability dynamically, you might want to add the Slot Validation component to the nest. Alternatively, just using a tag or Tag Predicate is fine.

Rendering[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#rendering "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This section covers the various components you can use to adjust certain rendering aspects of Accessories.

### Rendering Override[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#rendering-override "Permanent link")

Any equippable ItemStack (or Accessory) can have a component called `accessories:render_override`, which allows you to force enable/disable the default renderer or the armor renderer.

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-4-1) { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-4-2)     "accessories:render_override": { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-4-3)         "default_render_override": false, [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-4-4)         "armor_render_override": true [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-4-5)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-4-6) }`

| Field | Usage |
| --- | --- |
| `"default_render_override"` | An optional boolean value indicating if the default render should be used |
| `"armor_render_override"` | An optional boolean value indicating if the armor render should be used |

### Rendering Transformations[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#rendering-transformations "Permanent link")

For any Accessory that uses the default renderer: It is possible to use the `render_transformations` data component to adjust the positioning, rotation, and scale of the rendering. Some examples are wearing a block as a hat, or placing an item on your arm.

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-5-1) { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-5-2)     "accessories:render_transformations": { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-5-3)         "disable_default_translations": true, [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-5-4)         "transformations": [ [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-5-5)             { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-5-6)                 "type": "translation", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-5-7)                 "value": [-25, 0, 5] [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-5-8)             }, [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-5-9)             { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-5-10)                 "type": "axis_rotation", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-5-11)                 "value": { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-5-12)                     "angle": 90, [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-5-13)                     "axis": [1, 0, 1], [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-5-14)                 } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-5-15)             } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-5-16)         ] [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-5-17)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-5-18) }`

#### Transformations[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#transformations "Permanent link")

TranslationRaw RotationAxis RotationScaleTransform ToMatrix

Translates the given rendering position based on the provided offset `Vector`.

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-6-1) { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-6-2)     { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-6-3)         "type": "translation", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-6-4)         "value": [-25, 0, 5] [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-6-5)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-6-6) }`

The `"value"` should be a vector with the offset being in the `x`, `y`, and `z` format.

Rotates the given rendering based on the given `Quarternion` provided.

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-7-1) { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-7-2)     { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-7-3)         "type": "raw_rotation", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-7-4)         "value": [-0.323, 0.111, 0, 0.1232] [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-7-5)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-7-6) }`

The `"value"` should be a vector with the rotation being in the `x`, `y`, `z`, and `w` format.

Rotates the given rendering based on `Angle` (In Degrees) and `Axis` vector to rotate around.

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-8-1) { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-8-2)     { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-8-3)         "type": "axis_rotation", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-8-4)         "value": { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-8-5)             "angle": 90, [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-8-6)             "axis": [1, 0, 1], [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-8-7)         } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-8-8)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-8-9) }`

The `"value"` needs to be in the structured format with an `Angle` in **Degrees**, and an `Axis` vector in the `x`, `y`, and `z` format.

Scales the size of the rendering based on the given scale `Vector`.

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-9-1) { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-9-2)     { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-9-3)         "type": "scale", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-9-4)         "value": [-25, 0, 5] [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-9-5)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-9-6) }`

The `"value"` should be a vector with the offset being in the `x`, `y`, and `z` format.

Transforms the Rendering to the targeted `ModelPart` name based on the raw positioning `Vector` or specific `Side` of the part.

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-10-1) { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-10-2)     { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-10-3)         "type": "axis_rotation", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-10-4)         "value": { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-10-5)             "model_part": "head", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-10-6)             "raw_normal": [1, 1, 1], [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-10-7)         } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-10-8)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-10-9) }`

The `"value"` requires a `ModelPart` in string format and either the positioning (`"raw_normal"`) `Vector` as discussed within [Rendering API](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/rendering_api/#transformation-methods)
 or a specific `Side` (`"side"`) to translate the rendering to for the given part.

Applies a precomputed matrix to transform the renderer.

`[](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-11-1) { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-11-2)     { [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-11-3)         "type": "axis_rotation", [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-11-4)         "value": [ [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-11-5)             0.99985, -0.01745, 0.00030, 1.00000,   [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-11-6)             0.01745, 0.99970, -0.01745, 1.00000,  [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-11-7)             -0.00000, 0.01745, 0.99985, 1.00000, [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-11-8)             0.00000, 0.00000, 0.00000, 1.00000 [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-11-9)         ] [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-11-10)     } [](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/accessories/developer/itemstack_components/#__codelineno-11-11) }`

The `"value"` is a list of 16 doubles, representing the values of a 4x4 grid `Matrix`.

* * *

Last update: 2024-12-26

# How to build a Forge - Wisp Forest Docs

 

[Skip to content](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/alloy-forgery/building-a-forge/#forge-controller)

How to build a Forge
====================

_Up to date as of 2.0.22_

You can currently make an Alloy Forge out of 5 materials: Bricks, Stone Bricks, Blackstone, Deepslate, and End Stone. Alloy Forges are dynamically generated. You can add more of these through data, which is explained [on this page.](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/alloy-forgery/defining-a-forge.md)

The basic shape of a forge looks like this:  
![an image showing how to construct an Alloy Forge in 3 steps. Layer one is a 3x3 base. Layer two is the forge controller block in the front, and one block on each side, leaving the corners and the middle empty. Step three is the same as step two, but with a block instead of a controller](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/assets/alloy-forgery/forge_structure.png)

It has a 3x3 bottom, and is shaped like a chimney. You can put more blocks around it, even covering the top.

Forge Controller[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/alloy-forgery/building-a-forge/#forge-controller "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Forge controller is crafted from the respective material of the forge tier with a blast furnace in the middle:

![](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/assets/alloy-forgery/froge_controller_recipe.png)

### Tiers and Materials[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/alloy-forgery/building-a-forge/#tiers-and-materials "Permanent link")

Tiers are important for making recipes harder to make, or to make them more efficient.

Mods and modpacks can add their own Alloy Forges, but by default you can make a Forge out of the following materials:

*   Stone Bricks (Tier 1)
*   Bricks (Tier 1)
*   Polished Blackstone (Tier 2)
*   Deepslate Bricks (Tier 2)
*   Prismarine (Tier 2)
*   End Stone Bricks (Tier 3)

### Fuels[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/alloy-forgery/building-a-forge/#fuels "Permanent link")

A forge can by default be fueled by vanilla materials. Currently they accept the following list:

*   Coal and Blocks of Coal
*   Charcoal
*   Blaze Rods
*   Lava Bucket

For more information on how to add recipes and fuels, [go to this page.](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/alloy-forgery/adding-recipes-and-fuels.md)

Automation[¶](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/alloy-forgery/building-a-forge/#automation "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

As of Alloy Forgery 2.0.0 automation has been improved. You can now finally use hoppers to automate alloy forging. ![](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/assets/alloy-forgery/forge_hoppers_example.png)

Faster Transfer Method

You can also use a Hopper Minecart instead of a regular hopper. Modded transfer methods might not be supported.

* * *

As of Alloy Forgery 2.0.8 hoppers will automatically stop inserting items when it is forging. In larger contraptions, or older versions of the mod, you might want to use Redstone in order to automate them more effectively.  
![An image showing a comparator outputting a signal from a Forge Controller block into a Redstone lamp.](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/assets/alloy-forgery/forge_comparator_example.png)  
For this you can use a comparator on the Forge Controller. It even supports putting the comparator **_inside_** the Forge.

* * *

Last update: 2024-05-23

[Back to top](https://docs.wispforest.io/legacy/alloy-forgery/building-a-forge/#)
